League of Nations Adjourns to May; Locarno Negotiations Deadlocked; German Representative Returns Home Tomorrow for Consultations; Counterproposal to Be Submitted After Elections 22

London: Germany's response to Britain, France, and Belgium has now been extended to March 31, the second day after the German general election, before being formally submitted. The Locarno Pact negotiations have been temporarily prevented from collapsing. Hitler's special envoy, Ribbentrop, submitted a note to British Foreign Secretary Eden today, stating that Germany will submit detailed proposals but resolutely refuses to accept any proposals that harm Germany's equal rights and honor. (24th National Telegram)

London: The Council of the League of Nations held a closed-door meeting this afternoon, passing a resolution thanking the Locarno powers (Britain, France, Belgium, and Italy) for their efforts to maintain peace and expressing the opinion that while the Locarno signatory states are still in talks, the Council should suspend action. It then requested that the Locarno powers keep the Council informed of the progress of the talks at any time, before adjourning indefinitely. It was also decided that as soon as the situation is suitable for further consideration of the issues raised by the Belgian and French governments, the chairman should convene a meeting of the Council in Geneva. Dr. Dikhoff, a foreign ministry advisor, attended today's meeting as the German representative. (25th Reuters Telegram)

London: Judging from various indications, the discussion among the Locarno signatory states regarding the Rhineland issue seems likely to be stalled until mid-May. German representative Ribbentrop will meet with British Foreign Secretary Eden this afternoon to reiterate Germany's position. Ribbentrop will depart for Berlin on Friday but is expected to return to London next Tuesday with Hitler's counterproposal to the four-power memorandum. However, France will hold elections on May 3, and before the results of these elections are known, the various countries may not seriously study the German counterproposal. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini must wait until the efforts of the Spanish Prime Minister and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations regarding an Italo-Abyssinian settlement have yielded results before announcing Italy's position. Therefore, the various countries will not immediately seriously study the German counterproposal until Mussolini announces his position, which is why the discussion of the situation may be postponed until mid-May. French Minister Without Portfolio Flandin had a beneficial conversation with Eden this morning before returning to Paris, and Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov will also meet with the British Foreign Secretary this afternoon. (25th Reuters Telegram)

Content of German Reply: Rejection of Proposals Harming German Sovereignty 23

London: German representative Ribbentrop arrived here by plane from Berlin at 6:00 PM tonight. After a brief rest, he went to the office of the British Foreign Secretary to deliver the "Interim Reply" drafted by the German government to British Foreign Secretary Eden. The reply is divided into four parts, rejecting all proposals in the four-power draft that harm German sovereignty and damage German honor. The first section of the reply restates the German government's conclusion that the Franco-Soviet pact conflicts with the Locarno Pact in both legal and political terms. Therefore, the German government has no choice but to seek the restoration and integrity of its sovereignty within its borders. Germany's dispatch of troops into the Rhineland is not merely to reoccupy the region but is a preliminary preparation for building peace in Europe. This act of restoring sovereignty within its own borders cannot be separated from Germany's peace plan for a moment.

The second section of the reply solemnly states all the preliminary necessary conditions for building peace in Europe that the German government deems necessary. European countries should conclude a permanent agreement to guarantee peace in Europe, proceeding in a spirit of mutual understanding and respect for the principle of equal sovereignty of all countries. Governments should understand that the establishment of unequal treaties is naturally considered justified from the point of view of the beneficiary, but those who are harmed will certainly regard this as a portrayal of partiality and injustice and will do their best to abolish them. It is universally acknowledged that such treaties cannot last forever. Therefore, any treaty or agreement must be based on the principle of equality, concluded by the free will and awareness of each country, in order to hope for the support or sacrifice of the governments and peoples of each country. All countries must recognize this point, and then it will be easier to start solving future events. Germany has already completed this preliminary preparation by restoring the integrity of its sovereignty within its borders.

The third section of the reply states that, based on the above two sections, it can be seen that all the proposals in the four-power draft cannot contribute to building peace in Europe. If the German government accepts such proposals that harm German sovereignty, it will undoubtedly be condemned by the people. The German government will certainly not do so. Historical facts have already shown us that peace built on an unstable foundation will collapse. Therefore, the German government will refuse to accept all the proposals put forward by the Locarno powers, firmly believing that unless the peoples and their leaders of all countries have a sense of unconditional and lasting security and peace, all attempts to improve international social conditions will be ineffective. The peace plan put forward by Germany is based on this feeling.

The fourth section of the reply states the wishes of the German government and its people, saying that although Germany has refused to accept the proposals in the draft, it still hopes that the British government can put forward other more reasonable proposals to help resolve and clarify the current chaotic situation in Europe. Germany will naturally follow suit to do its part.

The reply concludes with a statement that the German government will have more concrete proposals and counterproposals to explain Germany's position in detail to the British government after the general election on March 31. (24th National Telegram)

British Authorities Announce: No Secret Agreements; France Insists Military Agreement Remains Valid 24

London: The White Paper on national defense plans, submitted by the government on the 3rd of this month, was passed by the House of Commons on the 10th of this month by a vote of 371 to 153. Today, the House of Lords passed it by a vote of 109 to 8. During the discussion, Lord Hailsham, the Lord Chancellor, speaking on behalf of the government, declared that no secret agreements had been concluded at the Locarno Conference and that Britain's obligations were limited to those already published in the draft agreement. (24th Havas Telegram)

London: French Ambassador to Britain Corbin recently visited Foreign Secretary Eden, lodging a protest on behalf of French Foreign Minister Flandin regarding the following two matters: 1. The draft agreement established at the Locarno Conference was disclosed by Britain before it had been approved by the countries concerned. 2. Eden explained this draft agreement in the House of Commons, saying that it was of a suggestive nature. Regarding the second point, Eden replied that his explanation only meant that the part of the draft agreement concerning the proposals to Germany was not of a definite nature, while the promise that Britain had made to France and Belgium, that if future negotiations broke down, Britain would come to the aid of France and Belgium, was unchangeable. (25th Havas Telegram)

London: Since the Locarno Treaty was rejected by Germany, French Minister Without Portfolio Flandin visited Foreign Secretary Eden this morning and issued a statement to him, saying that any expression of compromise that would endanger France's security in the future is not what France desires. It is unwilling to hear of Germany building defensive fortifications in the Rhineland region, which is no different from Britain's inability to recognize Germany having a base in the North Sea. (25th Havas Telegram)

Paris: The French political community believes that after Germany's entry into the Rhineland, the London Agreement of March 19 remains valid between Britain, France, and Belgium. Therefore, the general staffs of these three countries can begin consultations because countries that have not abandoned the Locarno Pact are still bound by its obligations and guarantees. The London Agreement stipulates: 1. The International Court of Justice in The Hague should determine whether the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty undermines the Locarno Pact as Germany claims. 2. An demilitarized zone should be established on the German side of the Franco-German border. 3. The British, French, and Belgian general staffs should consult on plans to protect this border. (25th Reuters Telegram)

Paris: Foreign Minister Flandin left for Yonne Province at 5:00 PM this afternoon to rest briefly. (Flandin will contest the general election in that province when the Chamber of Deputies holds its reelection on the 26th of next month.) He will continue to communicate with the Foreign Ministry during his absence from the capital so that he can rush back to the capital if necessary. Before his departure, Flandin paid a visit to Prime Minister Sarraut at 3:15 PM to discuss the attitude that France should adopt after Germany submitted its reply, a discussion that lasted an hour and a half. It was decided that France's attitude would not change, namely: 1. The Locarno Conference draft agreement is a whole; Germany must accept or reject it in its entirety. 2. France will not begin negotiations with Germany until this agreement is implemented. (24th Havas Telegram)

London: Since the Locarno Four-Power Agreement was rejected by Germany, French figures believe that the British and Italian representatives had previously sent letters to France and Belgium, declaring the mutual assistance measures that Britain and Italy, as guarantors of the Locarno Pact, should take, and that these should now be implemented. According to official sources here, the British government has never sent such letters to France and Belgium and will not do so until the Italian government has ratified the Locarno Four-Power Agreement. They said that the urgent task is to conduct negotiations among the countries concerned. On the one hand, Britain and Germany should conduct negotiations, and on the other hand, Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium should finalize the interim measures that have already been agreed upon. (25th Havas Telegram)

London: Since the German government rejected all the proposals in the draft Locarno Agreement, British officials commented on the German reply, believing that Germany's willingness to submit concrete proposals on March 31 proves that it has no intention of acting rashly, and that it is still possible for the country to show compromise after the House of Commons election. Foreign Secretary Eden has notified the delegations of Belgium, France, and Italy of the contents of the reply tonight. French Minister Without Portfolio Flandin is scheduled to meet with Eden tomorrow and fly back to France that afternoon to seek instructions from his government. (24th Havas Telegram)

Brussels: Minister of War Devèze recently declared to the National Defense Committee of the Chamber of Deputies that since the German army entered the Rhineland region and the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium concluded a military agreement, it is necessary to reform Belgium's conscription law. He therefore requested the Chamber of Deputies to promptly pass a bill authorizing the government to extend the term of military service in order to cope with the needs of border defense. The Chamber of Deputies will now organize a special committee to study the army reform plan prepared by the general staff. (24th Havas Telegram)

Brussels: The Chamber of Deputies has begun to discuss the draft agreement established at the Locarno Conference. Former Prime Minister Jaspar declared that the military agreement concluded by the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium is extremely important. (24th Havas Telegram)

Hitler's Doctrine: 1.5 Million Listeners 25

Berlin: Today, 20,000 people gathered in the newly completed "German Hall" in this city to listen quietly to Führer Hitler's election speech. The speech was also broadcast by radio to other gatherings with 200,000 listeners. The authorities also installed hundreds of loudspeakers on the streets and public squares of Berlin to broadcast Hitler's speech. It is estimated that the number of people gathering to listen in various places was around 1.5 million.

Hitler's speech began by recounting the domestic difficulties and hardships that Germany has suffered in the seventeen years since the signing of the Treaty of Versailles, as well as the oppression it has endured in foreign affairs. He then explained the current foreign policy adopted by the government, the purpose of which is to seek freedom and equality among nations and the integrity of domestic sovereignty. Any country that does not want Germany to achieve this goal is not worthy of talking about peace, because they do not want peace and do not trust peace. What they need is to exploit the interests of others to satisfy their own greed. He then explained Germany's current position on the issue of building peace in Europe, saying that it is impossible to seek temporary stability on the current foundation, and that it is necessary to thoroughly promote genuine understanding among nations and seek a fair adjustment of various disputes. He does not believe that there is truly a country in the world that wants its neighbors to be in a state of oppression forever. The reason is nothing more than that general dazzling and ostentatious opportunistic politicians mix the happiness of the entire nation with their personal feelings. As for the rejection of the four-power draft proposal, Hitler also declared that what we have lost in the past, we are now doing our best to recover. I am very grateful to God for enabling me to undertake this arduous task of fighting for the entire nation, but the countries of the world should understand that it is not that I personally am dissatisfied with the proposal and refuse to accept it, but that it is the trend of the public opinion of the entire German nation. We certainly do not want Germany's honor to suffer the slightest damage. Since we do not want to interfere in the affairs of others, nor do we want others to interfere in our affairs, we will naturally reject all oppressive and insulting demands without hesitation. Hitler then said that we have already offered a plan for peace to the world, and next Tuesday we will reiterate our proposals in the most perfect and clear way, so that the people of the world can know that what they think is impossible, we are now working hard to do. Therefore, I sincerely hope that the German people will show the people of the world in the general election on March 29 that this effort of Germany has the backing of the entire nation. At the end of his speech, Hitler reiterated the main point of his entire speech in the most concise words, saying, "Germany is willing to seek genuine peace with other countries, but any request by other countries to restrict Germany's freedom is absolutely unacceptable to Germany."

During Hitler's speech, every passionate and moving sentence aroused applause and cheers from the general audience, like an echo, the grandeur of which was unprecedented. (25th National Telegram)

Turkey Follows Germany's Lead: Demands Restoration of Sovereignty; Wants to Fortify the Dardanelles Strait 26

London: Turkey, in its capacity as a member of the Council of the League of Nations, formally notified the League of Nations today, demanding the right to fortify the Dardanelles Strait, the Bosphorus Strait, and the Sea of Marmara. These three places were previously Turkey's strategic areas before the European War. Now Turkey will abandon the annex to the Treaty of Lausanne that stipulates that Turkey will establish a demilitarized zone in the waterways for communication with Europe. The reason is that Germany has re-stationed troops in the Rhineland region, and Turkey can also follow suit and abandon the Treaty of Lausanne. (24th National Telegram)

London: The News Chronicle reports that since Germany abolished the Locarno Pact on the 7th of this month and dispatched troops into the Rhineland region, the situation has greatly changed. The Turkish government, in view of this, has decided to raise the issue of re-fortifying the Dardanelles Strait at any moment. Turkey has long been concerned about the Dardanelles Strait, which was stipulated by the Treaty of Lausanne in 1923 as not allowed to be fortified. When the Italo-Abyssinian dispute occurred, the British government contacted the countries along the Mediterranean coast in December of last year to discuss naval cooperation, and Turkey was also among them. At that time, Turkey believed that this was a rare opportunity and planned to take the opportunity to demand that the clause in the Treaty of Lausanne stipulating that the Dardanelles Strait should not be fortified be abolished. Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü Aras also discussed this matter with former French Prime Minister Laval, hoping that France would support Turkey's request. Later, because Germany already had the intention to demand the re-fortification of the Rhineland, the Turkish authorities believed that it would be inappropriate to raise the issue of the Dardanelles Strait and temporarily put the matter on hold. (25th Havas Telegram)

Italo-Austro-Hungarian Protocol: Establishment of a Consultation Mechanism for Cooperation 27

Rome: As a result of continuous consultations among the authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary, three protocols have been signed to supplement the shortcomings of the Three-Power Agreement of March 17, 1934. The main points are as follows:

(First item) The three governments decided to establish a permanent consultation mechanism to further strengthen cooperation among their countries.

(Second item) The three governments mutually agree that if any signatory state of this protocol conducts political negotiations with other countries on the Danube River basin issue, it should consult with the other two signatory states in advance. Otherwise, these negotiations shall not be conducted. The three governments also agreed that the economic relations between each signatory state and other countries in the Danube River basin should be further strengthened. Although this is expected, at present, other countries in the Danube River basin may not directly join the Italo-Austro-Hungarian Three-Power Agreement, but may only conclude bilateral agreements with it in order to develop mutual economic relations.

(Third item) The above-mentioned permanent consultation mechanism is composed of the foreign ministers of the three countries and should meet periodically at a time deemed appropriate by the three governments. (25th Havas Telegram)

Rome: According to reliable sources here, the treaty established by Italy, Austria, and Hungary has indirectly involved Czechoslovakia in the diplomatic network in Central Europe planned by Prime Minister Mussolini. One reason is that Czechoslovakia has agreed to purchase certain exports from Austria. Secondly, if a dispute occurs between Czechoslovakia and Germany, Italy promises to support Czechoslovakia diplomatically. Italy also promises to strongly encourage Hungary to participate in the future coordination of the people of the Danube River region. (24th National Telegram)

Anglo-American-French Naval Treaty Signed; US and UK Issue Statement Maintaining Equilibrium 28

London: Reliable sources indicate that the US Chief Delegate to the London Naval Conference, Davis, and British Foreign Secretary Eden exchanged documents today, continuing to uphold the principle of naval equality between the two countries. The significance of this statement is seen as an expression of cooperation between the US and UK amidst Japan's isolation. (National Telegram, 25th)

The London Naval Conference held a plenary session at 4:15 PM today in Queen Anne's Room at St. James's Palace. The chief representatives of the UK, France, and the United States signed the naval treaty. Italy, the various British Dominions, and India sent representatives to participate. Japan also sent Counselor Fujii and Naval Captain Fujita from its embassy in the UK as observers. The 1930 London Naval Conference and the recent extraordinary meeting of the 91st League of Nations Council were also held in this room, making it a place of historical significance. The room's pillars were painted white, complemented by deep red decorations, enhancing the clarity of the colors. The huge fireplace was filled with burning logs and coal smoke, creating a warm atmosphere. Paintings of George I through George III, along with many famous paintings, hung on the walls. Bright lights were suspended from the ceiling by golden chains, surrounded by forty candle-shaped electric lamps. Many wall lamps were also installed, creating a soft light. The conference table was horseshoe-shaped, with the chairman's seat in the middle, occupied by British Foreign Secretary Eden, the same seat that British Prime Minister Baldwin used during the opening of the naval conference. Seated opposite Eden, starting from the left end, were, in alphabetical order by country name, US Chief Delegate Davis, Delegate Rear Admiral Stanley, followed by representatives from Australia, Canada, France, the UK, India, Ireland, Italy, New Zealand, and the Union of South Africa. Other experts and advisors from each country sat behind the representatives in the second row. Japanese observers Fujii and Fujita sat behind the French experts. Only a few journalists were allowed to listen in the room, so microphones were placed on the conference table to transmit the speeches of each country's chief representative to the adjacent room for the majority of journalists to record. The agenda for today's meeting was divided into five items: The Chairman, British Foreign Secretary Eden, delivered a speech. The chief representatives of each country delivered speeches in alphabetical order by country name. They then signed the treaty in alphabetical order. The chief representatives of each country could express further opinions after signing. The Chairman announced the adjournment of the conference, using the phrase "the naval conference is now adjourned" rather than "closed," the same situation as at the end of the 1930 London Naval Conference, so that the naval conference would nominally remain in existence and could be reopened at any time in the future. The naval treaty signed was divided into three parts. The first part concerned the procedures for exchanging shipbuilding programs and other information among the signatory countries. The second part concerned the qualitative restrictions on various types of ships. The third part concerned safeguard clauses. As for the measures to restrict submarine warfare, a protocol will be signed through diplomatic channels at a later date to regulate them. In addition, regarding the issue of prohibiting fortifications on Pacific islands, the Japanese government, through Counselor Fujii of its embassy in the UK, notified the British government, stating that Japan was prepared to extend the term of the measures stipulated in Article 19 of the Washington Naval Treaty. However, as of now, the United States has not submitted a reply to the UK, so this issue may not be resolved in the near future. (Havas Dispatch, 25th)

Hirota Receives Foreign Correspondents; Explains Japan's Domestic and Foreign Policies; Active Externally, Gradual Internally; Fiscal Policy Avoids Shaking the National Economy; Naval Committee Established to Study Reform 30

Tokyo: Premier Hirota met with the foreign press corps at the Prime Minister's official residence at 4:00 PM on the 25th. In a conversational manner, he clarified the Japanese government's foreign policy as follows: "Regarding the current cabinet's domestic and foreign policies, these were announced some days ago, and I believe you are all very familiar with them. The foundation of Japan's foreign policy was made clear in the Imperial Rescript when we announced our withdrawal from the League of Nations on March 27th of Showa 8 [1933]. In short, we must first ensure the stability of East Asia, and at the same time, in the spirit of harmony among all nations, conduct friendly relations with friendly countries. We sincerely hope to contribute further to the progress of international peace and the well-being of mankind. Relations between Japan and China will also gradually deepen. Therefore, we will establish normal relations between Japan, China, and Manchukuo, and promote their cooperation and collaboration. At the same time, we will further strengthen our long-standing goodwill with the United States, the Soviet Union, and other countries. We wish to fully implement our mission regarding the stability of East Asia. As for trade and economic issues, we must enhance Japan's economic needs and eliminate trade barriers and make adjustments. Therefore, in order to promote full progress in trade, we intend to work very hard." (Domei News Agency, 25th)

Tokyo: Premier Hirota, accompanied by Director of the Information Bureau, Amano, met with the press corps from the UK, US, France, Germany, and the Soviet Union on the 25th for forty minutes, discussing foreign and domestic policies. In addition to issuing a statement in a conversational style, the following is a record of the question-and-answer session:

(Press Corps Question) What is meant by independent and proactive diplomacy?

(Premier Hirota Answer) The so-called independence refers to exercising independent diplomacy. In the past, there has been a tendency to be slow in resolving pending issues. Therefore, in the future, we intend to work on proactive measures to resolve pending issues with various countries.

(Question) Regarding the importance of Japan-China relations, what policies will be adopted in the future?

(Answer) This remains the most important foreign policy issue. Therefore, the Japanese government intends to be extremely cautious in adjusting relations between the two countries.

(Question) Does the Premier still intend to promote the Three Principles for China presented at the 68th Diet as before?

(Answer) My speech in the Diet cannot be changed. The Three Principles are the fundamental policy for adjusting Japan-China issues, and they are not only for the benefit of Japan but also take into account the interests of friendly countries. Therefore, the policy is aimed at adjusting the interests of both sides.

(Question) Mr. Molotov recently told the foreign press corps in Moscow that relations between Japan and the Soviet Union have improved. What is the situation?

(Answer) I have seen this in news articles and I feel it is good. Japan has always worked to maintain friendly relations, but the Soviet side sometimes says that Japan-Soviet relations are dangerous, and sometimes they say they are improving. In short, this is their point of view. Japan's attitude has not changed in any way. Now that Mr. Molotov is gradually understanding Japan's attitude, it is very gratifying.

(Question) Was the issue of purchasing Northern Sakhalin also mentioned? (At this point, the Premier looked at Mr. Nagi, the correspondent for the Soviet TASS news agency, and replied) Mr. Nagi knows this very well, please ask him.

(Press Corps Question) The current cabinet is said to be implementing domestic reforms, but the road ahead is difficult.

(Premier Hirota Answer) This issue is extremely difficult, but it is like walking the path of life, there will inevitably be ripples. We intend to make great efforts to break down accumulated malpractices.

(Question) What is the content of the so-called renewal of education? Is it intended to suppress foreign ideas?

(Answer) In the future, we should certainly absorb foreign culture, but we must review whether it is truly suitable for the conditions in Japan. (Domei News Agency, 25th)

Tokyo: Finance Minister Baba held a meeting of local tax bureau, supervisory bureau, customs, and monopoly bureau chiefs at the Central Conference Hall at 9:30 AM on the 25th, expressing the following about financial policy: "The traditional financial policies have not been able to adapt to the current era, so they must be changed. In my opinion, due to the implementation of national policies, it will not be possible to reduce expenditures in the future, and state expenses are likely to expand further. Relying on a deficit bond policy is definitely not a good method. Therefore, it is necessary to revise the tax system and implement tax increases to strengthen the financial foundation. However, the method of implementation should avoid rapid changes that would damage the national economy, which is the foundation of finance. Furthermore, the tax increase plan must be carried out in conjunction with policies to promote trade and industry, in order to restore the national economic power in other areas." (Domei News Agency, 25th)

Tokyo: In response to the Hirota cabinet's renewal of national policy, the naval authorities have newly established a Naval System Investigation Committee, which convened its first general meeting on the 23rd. Within this committee, three subcommittees were established for policy, institutional reform, and budget, and they have begun active investigation and research. Navy Minister Nagano convened the head of the Investigation Committee, Director General Hasegawa, Bureau Chief of Naval Affairs, Toyoda, and Bureau Chief of Accounting, Murakami, in the ministry conference room at 1:30 PM on the 25th, to instruct the members on the policy of the Investigation Committee. He stated in brief: "In light of the domestic and international situation, we must take a cautious attitude and attempt to reform the naval system. Therefore, investigation and research must be carried out meticulously, and we must strive for comprehensive plans. At the same time, concrete plans must be implemented according to their urgency." The three subcommittees, centered on the two committee chiefs Toyoda and Murakami, are first collecting basic data to establish concrete plans, and will adjust them as soon as possible, aiming to start formal activities as early as April to promote their success. (Domei News Agency, 25th)

Tokyo: The first conference of army commanders and division commanders since Land Minister Terauchi took office will be held at the Land Minister's official residence for five days starting on the 7th of next month. At that time, Land Minister Terauchi will explain in detail the entire picture of the 上决事伴 [likely a typo, should be 上级指示事項 Superior Instructions] and instruct on the army's highest policies for the future. Therefore, all quarters are paying close attention. The main points of the important instructions are as follows: "The 上决 [likely a typo, should be 上级 Upper Level] rebellion and the violent acts of the rebel army have greatly disrupted the unified command and violated military discipline. For the sake of building the Imperial Army's guiding principles and prestige, it is deeply regrettable. The army must now overcome all difficulties, eradicate such incidents, and reassure the Emperor. To make a fresh start and rebuild the Imperial Army, the entire army must unite with the greatest determination, stake their lives, and move forward together. Therefore, we expect the strengthening of the spiritual education of each unit and the thoroughness of moral education. Subordinates must not be confused by rumors and gossip, and we must strictly prohibit reckless actions. As for disciplinary actions and punishments, the laws are strict and impartial, and there will be no leniency. However, when applying the law, we must pay attention to the current domestic situation, which needs to be corrected and reformed. The military central department, together with the reform of national policy, will move forward together within the Control Department." (Dentsu, 25th)

US Election Campaign; Republican Party Nominates Presidential Candidates 31

Washington: The Republican Party today launched a campaign in the Midwest to select presidential candidates, attacking the New Deal and protecting the interests of the business community and private individuals. Judging from the situation in the eastern states, it seems that the large commercial sectors on the Atlantic coast are eager to support the Republican Party and believe that Kansas Governor Landon is the most promising presidential candidate. At the same time, the capitalists who provide the party's election expenses all believe that Landon is more likely to defeat President Roosevelt than Chicago publisher Knox. However, if Knox can make a final effort before the party holds its election convention, those in the East who support Landon may be willing to switch their support to Knox as a candidate. According to knowledgeable observers, the eastern states do not show much enthusiasm for Senator Borah's radical opposition to the New Deal. The northeastern states on the Atlantic coast are not very concerned about the Republican Party's presidential candidate, but their desire for President Roosevelt to leave the White House is very urgent. (National Telegram, 24th)

Washington: The movement to nominate Republican presidential candidates has two very distinct developments: 1. Borah has entered the primary campaign in New Jersey. 2. The position of Kansas Governor Landon is also becoming clearer. Although Landon has stated that his state affairs are busy and that he has decided to abandon participating in the campaign in order to maintain party harmony, the faction led by Republican Senator Pope has decided to support Landon as the presidential candidate. Therefore, the divisions within the Republican Party are now very clear. Borah's faction is the progressive faction, while Landon is the conservative faction. It is reported that the Republican primary campaign in New Jersey will be held on May 19th. (National Telegram, 24th)

Song Zheyuan Discusses the Recent Situation of North China Diplomacy 73

Always Uphold Sincerity and Peace in Dealing with Friendly Nations. Determined to Exert Utmost Efforts to Defend Territory and Interests. Determine a Plan to Seek National Salvation from Ourselves.

Baoding Correspondence: Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and concurrently Chairman of Hebei Province, recently delivered an important speech, frankly discussing issues such as North China's diplomacy. He stated, "Because I have been away from the province for a long time, I have returned to Baoding to preside over all government affairs. I originally planned to stay in Baoding for a few days before going on tour to various counties in southern Hebei to inquire about the suffering of the people. However, due to time constraints, it is difficult to go, and I have decided to suspend the tour for the time being. After questioning the county magistrates in Baoding, I will return to Ping, or go on tour again when I come to the province next time. Since recent years, various undertakings in Hebei Province have been extremely corrupt. Everything from telephones to road administration has become unusable. When I decided to go to Shandong, I reached the border between the two provinces and saw that the roads in the two provinces were very different. The Shandong territory was flat and wide, while the Hebei territory was rugged and uneven. Telephone poles in Shandong were as high as thirty or forty feet, while those in Hebei were only a little over ten feet. Such things must be thoroughly revitalized and realistically rectified. I have now ordered the Department of Construction to take charge of the matter in order to facilitate transportation and enhance the appearance. After the rampancy of the communist bandits in western Shanxi, the military situation for suppressing bandits has become tense day by day. The communist bandits also have the intention of infiltrating Taiyuan. The Shanxi army has now deployed solid defenses in Taiyuan, so they will probably not succeed. If the Shanxi bandits fail to infiltrate Taiyuan, they may flee north to the Sui territory and will not flee east to Hebei Province, because the province is a vast plain where bandits cannot hide. Moreover, heavy troops are stationed at various passes on the western border of Hebei, so even if they come, it will be difficult to invade. Red Spear Society bandits and communist bandits in southern Hebei have been surrounded by troops, and political forces have been used to actively eliminate them. It is hoped that there will be no worries. The issue of North China diplomacy has not progressed since the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, and all kinds of issues are in a state of stagnation. It seems that the Japanese side has not clearly decided on a definite diplomatic policy towards North China. Recently, the Japanese officials responsible for North China have also been transferred, so all issues have become unresolved. As for our North China authorities, we have decided to exert our utmost efforts in everything under the principle of defending territory and interests, and we have formulated appropriate steps to decide to seek national salvation from ourselves. We hope to create a new atmosphere within five years, so that the main policies of politics, diplomacy, military affairs, and construction can be brought into line. Then there is hope for self-rescue and national salvation. The diplomatic policy of North China is still to deal with everything with an attitude of 'peace and sincerity.' I will meet with Japanese Ambassador Arita after he comes to North China, but it has not been decided. If it is necessary to have a meeting at that time, I also plan to express to him the North China authorities' ardent hope for maintaining peace in East Asia, hoping that both sides will achieve genuine mutual assistance and cooperation. The issue of abolishing the puppet organization in eastern Hebei is also in a state of stagnation. In short, I am responsible for defending the territory of North China. Internally, I must thoroughly rectify everything and realistically revitalize the national spirit in order to seek self-determination. Externally, I will always uphold the principle of sincerity and peace and maintain peace in East Asia with friendly nations. In addition, in order to strengthen the local capacity to defend against bandits in Hebei Province, it has been decided to divide ten security zones, each with a commander, to effectively lead the people to overcome difficulties and defend themselves. The Baojia system is a facility to build the ability of the people themselves organization, so it was decided to order all counties to still apply the mandatory system, no longer set up additional recruitment officer, causing additional people's burden, and the province is financially strapped, and the people's economy has also become bankrupt. At present, in order to reduce the burden on the people, it has been decided to exempt all additional donations. Strict orders have been issued to all counties to handle the matter conscientiously, and it is estimated that additional donations can be reduced by as much as 2 million yuan per year. As for the provincial treasury itself, there have been huge deficits over the years. The province's annual income is only over 14 million yuan, while the annual expenditure budget is over 19 million yuan. Income cannot cover expenditure, and there is always a shortfall. I have decided to allocate and apply the province's budget based on the original income item of over 14 million yuan, and strive to do so on the principle of economizing expenditures. The Poor People's Association in western Hebei is harassing the local area. According to investigations, most of them are salt farmers who are unable to pay taxes and go astray. The tax police in the Pingxiang area have now been withdrawn, and personnel have been sent to study the geology of the area, hoping to scientifically improve the barren salt land so that it can be used to grow farmland. Once the people have fields to cultivate, they will naturally not embark on dangerous paths again. Regarding the dispute over the exchange of counties between Hebei and Henan, the local people in this province have been arguing fiercely, and for the sake of the safety of North China, we cannot ignore the river defenses along the river. Therefore, I have forwarded the petition of the people of this province to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior to revoke the previous proposal. If it is inconvenient to change due to the fact that the Executive Yuan has already passed the resolution, we must also take the Yellow River as the boundary and seek a compromise." (24th)

Dongzhuang Yellow River Breach Expected to Close Soon 74

The Closing Project is Extremely Rapid. Water from the Breach Flows into the Old River.

Jinan Correspondence: The closing project of the Dongzhuang Yellow River breach is progressing rapidly even in the dead of winter. The encroachment project began on January 1 and was completed on the 19th of this month. A total of 31 sections of the west dike, 62 meters in length, and 9 sections of the east dike, 174 meters in length, were constructed. The breach is now only 39.3 meters wide. Side dikes are also being built, each 10 meters shorter than the main dikes on the east and west sides. Since the evening of the 19th, willow mattresses have been thrown from the heads of the two dikes, and earth cabinets have been filled between the two dikes. The willow mattress workers work in shifts, day and night, without rest. Kong Xiangrong, acting chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, along with all the staff, Wang Yujun, etc., are supervising the work on the dam day and night, under great tension. A willow mattress can be thrown every ten to fifteen minutes. Three hundred willow mattresses are thrown from the heads of both dikes day and night. As of the evening of the 23rd, the west dike had been thrown 8 meters out of the water, and the east dike had been thrown 6.5 meters. The breach is now only 25 meters long. The river water in the breach is about 10 meters deep at the deepest point. That evening, the northeast wind was very strong, which was quite beneficial to the work. Therefore, Kong accelerated the work by taking the opportunity, and it is expected that all the water can be discharged by the evening of the 24th, and the side dikes will be used to occupy and close the gap. Ten cabinets will be built on the dam, and then hemp bags filled with stone and earth will be thrown in front of the willow mattresses to seal the air, and the closing will be successful. If there are no special changes, it can be completed as scheduled on the 25th. A total of six diversion channels are being controlled, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, and 6, above the breach, to divert the water from the breach. The fourth channel is the Lishun Village North Diversion Channel, below the breach, directly opposite the lower mouth of the third diversion channel. Removing the river bend can make the river water flow smoothly. After starting to throw willow mattresses on the evening of the 19th, the water in the breach gradually increased. On the morning of the 20th, the five and six diversion channels were opened, and the water situation stabilized immediately. It rose again in the afternoon, and when the second diversion channel was reopened, a southwest wind blew strongly, which was in the right direction for the fourth diversion channel. Soldiers and laborers were mobilized, and the channel was opened by taking the opportunity. The riverhead had already automatically washed away a part, so it was opened smoothly. Then the third diversion channel was also opened. The water was surging and the situation was very good. On the 22nd, the total river flow was measured to be 670 cubic meters per second. The breach still flowed 520 cubic meters per second, while the old river and diversion channel flowed 150 cubic meters per second. On the 23rd, the water in the diversion channel increased even more. The fourth diversion channel has reached a depth of four meters. Therefore, although the breach is gradually narrowing, the water level has not risen. The first diversion channel was opened the earliest, and it has recently merged with the old river to form a river surface more than 100 feet wide. According to the evaluation of the Engineering Office, the completion of this diversion channel not only fundamentally reduces the water in the breach but also straightens the river channel, and the improvement of the river course has also achieved considerable success in the fundamental river management plan. Kong Xiangrong has now sent a telegram to Minister Kong, Secretary-General Qin Fen of the Economic Commission, Inspector Fang Juehui, and Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu, reporting on the opening of the diversion channel and the preparation for the breach closing project. (24th)

—Simultaneously Construct the Qin-Tao Branch Line of the Gansu-Sichuan Road—

Lanzhou Correspondence: Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong has been actively implementing measures to clarify officialdom, rectify tax collection, and promote various construction projects. Later, Wu Boqiong and Li Shiduo, technical specialists from the provincial government, were sent to re-survey and confirm the cost, which was submitted to the 386th meeting of the provincial affairs conference for resolution. Approval was granted for the repairs, and the labor and material costs were allocated as requested. The Gansu-Sichuan Highway is an important thoroughfare for transportation between Gansu Province and Sichuan Province. Although the Department of Construction has sent teams to survey, it has not been built due to a lack of funds. Chairman Yu resolutely raised over 140,000 yuan from the very tight funds to first repair the Qin-Tao branch line of the Gansu-Sichuan Highway in order to lay a foundation. This was also approved by the provincial affairs conference, and the Finance Department was ordered to allocate the funds.

Jiangxi Province Land Consolidation Plan 76

Divide into Nine Zones, Five Phases, Scheduled to Be Completed in Eight Years. Total Funding of Over 10,680,000 Yuan Required.

Nanchang Correspondence: The land consolidation plan in this province has been adopted since May 21st with the use of aerial surveys, starting with a pilot project in Nanchang County. By January 23rd, the aerial surveying of all fields and mu in the county was completed, and 8,615 original land maps were produced. The Land Bureau sent personnel to investigate and confirmed that the aerial surveying test had achieved considerable results. The Land Bureau then formulated a land consolidation plan for the entire province to promote it throughout the province. The 82 counties including Xinjian were divided into five zones and consolidated in five phases. The first zone is Xinjian and 9 other counties, the second zone is Ji'an and 10 other counties, the third zone is Poyang and 14 other counties, the fourth zone is Pengze and 22 other counties, and the fifth zone is Guangze and 22 other counties. It is estimated to be completed in eight years, requiring a total of 10,681,195 yuan in land consolidation fees. This has now been approved by the Provincial Affairs Conference. The contents of the plan are as follows:

Division of Zones

The province's 83 counties, excluding Nanchang County, which has completed operations during the aerial survey pilot project, are divided into five zones: Zone 1: Xinjian, Anyi, Jinxian, Qingjiang, Dongxiang, Fengcheng, Gao'an, Linchuan, Xingan, Jinxi, and ten other counties; Zone 2: Ji'an, Jishui, Yongfeng, Xiajiang, Xinyu, Taihe, Chongren, Yihuang, Le'an, Anfu, Wan'an, and eleven other counties; Zone 3: Poyang, Yugan, Shangrao, Guixi, Yiyang, Yujiang, Hengfeng, Leping, Dexing, Fuliang, Yushan, Guangfeng, Qianjiang, Wannian, Wuyuan, and fifteen other counties; Zone 4: Pengze, Hukou, Jiujiang, Xingzi, Duchang, Ruichang, De'an, Yongxiu, Wuning, Jing'an, Fengxin, Xiushui, Tonggu, Yifeng, Shanggao, Wanzai, Fenyi, Yichun, Pingxiang, Lianhua, Yongxin, Ninggang, Suichuan, and twenty-three other counties; Zone 5: Guangze, Zixi, Lichuan, Nancheng, Nanfeng, Guangchang, Shicheng, Ningdu, Ruijin, Xingguo, Lingdu, Ganxian, Nankang, Xinfeng, Shangyou, Chongyi, Dayu, Xunwu, Huichang, Anyuan, Dingnan, Qiannan, Longnan, and twenty-three other counties.

Aerial Survey Operations

The Jiangxi Aerial Survey Team will first photograph the shapes of each land plot on the film within each county's area, and then measure the longitudinal and transverse triangulation locks to correct the re-photographs and enlarge them into 1/1000 photo maps. They will then take them to the field for drawing, creating the original land map. The Jiangxi Provincial Land Bureau will conduct field surveys based on the original land map, including area measurement, map production, and record creation. The land registration offices in each county and the land registration offices in each district will then handle land registration. The various types of operations are described separately below: (A) Aerial surveying is divided into the following five items: Aerial photography uses an aerial camera with an 18 cm square film to capture 1/10,000 scale negatives, overlapping by 1/3 from front to back and 1/2 from side to side, to provide the basis for enlarging the original land map. Large mountains and lakes without farmland will not be photographed to save time and money. Control uses theodolites and multi-image cameras to measure longitudinal and transverse triangulation locks, with a distance of 10 kilometers between each lock. The entire area is divided into several small areas according to natural boundaries such as large mountains and rivers. Each small area starts counting from a new point to avoid accumulating errors. Correction corrects the 1/10,000 negatives with control points and enlarges them into 1/2,500 scale photos. The negatives without control points are corrected based on ground features. The map outlines are then divided and map numbers are assigned. Re-photography enlarges the corrected 1/2,500 scale photos to 1/1,000 scale photo maps using the straight-line re-photography method. Drawing takes the photo maps to the field to identify the boundaries, land categories, and names of cities, towns, villages, roads, mountains, and rivers of each land plot, and records them in detail. The forests, shaded areas, and unclear parts of the photos are then surveyed and mapped to create the original land map. (B) Land registration is divided into the following five items: Surveying first determines the boundaries of the county, district, and village near the local area based on the scope of the county, district, and village determined in the original aerial survey map. Then, based on the original land map, it divides the land price zones, determines the standard land price, and submits it to the land price estimation committee for estimation, creating and publishing a land price zone map. Area measurement uses a planimeter or the three-oblique method to measure and determine the area of each land plot and compiles the total area to create various statistical tables. Mapping copies the original land map to create the land map and reduces the total map, as well as a list map of counties, districts, and villages. Record creation compiles the land register and land tax household register based on the registered land ownership and estimated land price. The land register records the name, address, land category, area, land price, and annual tax payable of the owner of each land plot. Registration establishes a county land registration office in the county where the surveying and compilation have been completed to manage land registration matters throughout the county. Land registration offices are established in districts where surveying, area measurement, and mapping have been completed. Land registration is handled within a time limit, and land ownership certificates are issued for each land plot, with land maps attached.

Consolidation Period

The consolidation period required for each zone is estimated as follows: Zone 1, aerial surveying started in July 23rd of the Republic of China, completed in June 25th, and consolidation completed in June 26th; Zone 2, aerial surveying started in July 25th, completed in June 26th, and consolidation completed in June 28th; Zone 3, aerial surveying started in July 26th, completed in June 27th, and consolidation completed in June 29th; Zone 4, aerial surveying started in July 27th, completed in June 28th, and consolidation completed in June 30th; Zone 5, aerial surveying started in July 28th, completed in June 29th, and consolidation completed in June 31st. From July 23rd of the Republic of China, when aerial surveying of the land maps of the eleven counties including the first zone, Xinjian, began, to June 31st, when the farmland repair of the entire province was completed, a total of eight years are required.

Funding Required

Based on the needs of the operations, the estimated amount of funding required for each zone is as follows: Zone 1, Xinjian, and ten other counties have a land area of 74,584 square li, including 6,793,224 mu of farmland, requiring 2,052,702 yuan for consolidation fees and 466,000 yuan for aerial surveying start-up fees, for a total of 2,518,702 yuan. Zone 11, Poyang and fifteen other counties have a land area of 110,962 square li, including 6,753,853 mu of farmland, requiring a total of 2,026,117 yuan for consolidation fees. Zone 4, Jiujiang and twenty-two other counties have a land area of 131,813 square li, including 6,484,361 mu of farmland, requiring a total of 1,992,019 yuan for consolidation fees. Zone 5, Ganxian and twenty-two other counties have a land area of 142,453 square li, including 1,330,245 mu of farmland, requiring a total of 1,921,617 yuan for consolidation fees. The total land consolidation fee required for the eighty-two counties including Xinjian (excluding Nanchang County) is 10,681,195 yuan. This funding will be paid from the land registration certificate fee revenue of each county.

Guangdong Provincial Department Requests Funds to Run Relief Programs 77

—Allocated to Eighty-Two County Bureaus—

Guangzhou Correspondence: In Guangdong's three-year administration plan, great emphasis is placed on relief programs. Since its implementation, it has been quite effective. However, there have been cases where, due to local poverty and difficulty in raising funds, the relief homes and civilian hospitals that should be established urgently have been delayed for a long time. Because rural areas are on the brink of bankruptcy, industry and commerce are struggling, disasters have not ceased, and there are more and more poor people in need of relief in various counties, the Provincial Civil Affairs Department Minister Lin Yizhong, in view of this, previously requested approval from the provincial treasury to allocate 100,000 yuan, and together with the Department's saved relief funds of more than 60,000 yuan, distribute them to the poorer counties, with 4,000 yuan to the larger ones and 1,000 yuan to the smaller ones, ordering them to be saved as a relief fund. Since then, after deciding to allocate supplementary subsidies, the Civil Affairs Department has continued to urge the effective implementation of the program. The relief homes and civilian hospitals in various counties have been prepared and established one after another, but it is still not universal. Recently, it was again requested that the provincial government allocate as much as possible 200,000 yuan from the Civil Affairs Department's saved funds and the saved funds of the surveying team when it was also handling land administration to be distributed to various county bureaus to enrich the relief fund, so that the income from interest is increased, and the power of relief is greater. It is planned to allocate 4,000 yuan to each of the eleven counties, including Lianping, for a total of 44,000 yuan; 3,000 yuan to each of the twenty-one counties, including Rao Ping, for a total of 63,000 yuan; 2,000 yuan to each of the thirty-six counties, including Haifeng, for a total of 72,000 yuan; and 1,500 yuan to each of the fourteen counties, including Guangning, for a total of 21,000 yuan, for a total allocation of 200,000 yuan to eighty-two county bureaus.

Baoshan: General Investigation of Opium Offenders Ends 78

The general situation of Baoshan County Magistrate Zhang Mingjing's handling of the general investigation of opium offenders has been recorded in previous reports. It is now known that the county's general investigation ended on the 20th. The total number of offenders reported was 215, of whom 58 were released on bail by autonomous personnel, 65 were at large, and 92 were detained by the county government for interrogation. It is also known that of the 92 people detained by the county, 50 were verified to be free of addiction and drugs and have been released. The remaining 42 people all admitted to private smoking, relapse, private sale, or were verified to be addicted and have drugs in their bodies, so they will be sentenced in accordance with the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Opium Prohibition. It is reported that Provincial Guidance Committee member Ning Bojin, because the county's general investigation has come to an end, revisited each district yesterday with Secretary Bai Mingdao, Section Chief Fang of the Fourth Section, and Group Chief Tang of the Public Security Group to inspect the situation and gave detailed instructions on the future policy of opium prohibition. It is reported that Ning will return to the province tomorrow to report on his mission.

Songjiang: St. Joseph's Hospital Benefits the Poor 79

Lu Bohong, a great philanthropist in Shanghai, has spared no effort in handling charitable undertakings throughout his life and is admired by people at home and abroad. During the two wars of Jiazi and Dingmao, Lu established reception centers and rear hospitals in the St. Joseph's Hospital he privately founded, which benefited many. Now, in view of rural bankruptcy, Lu has specially added free wards to St. Joseph's Hospital and increased the number of places in the nursing home in order to relieve the poor. The directors of the Songjiang Red Cross have also vowed to collect donations from various philanthropists to make this a righteous act and benefit the poor. The people of the county admire this. The reelection of the county chamber of commerce has been announced.

County Chamber of Commerce Re-election Results 80

The County Chamber of Commerce held its re-election meeting today (the 25th). There were 335 members, and 301 attended. The county government sent District Chief Shen Fuyun to attend and supervise, and the county party headquarters sent Sun Shichi to provide guidance. The meeting was presided over by the chairman of the association, Zhu Yian, with formalities observed. More than ten proposals were discussed, followed by the re-election. The elected executive committee members were Jin Xianglin, Shi Jiepan, Yang Yunwen, Hu Bangqiao, Cai Shuming, Chen Shujun, Wu Zhizhong, and Shen Shuwen. The alternate executive committee members were Zhang Jiliang, Zhang Mengxing, Zhang Dehua, and four others, totaling seven. The elected supervisory committee members were Cai Guangyao, Yang Yunsheng, Shen Sinan, and Song Zhanquan. The alternate supervisors were Ding Liutai and two others, totaling three. The elected representatives to the Provincial Federation were Cai Guangyao, Zhu Yian, Yang Zhimin, and Zhang Jiliang.

Wuxi: Closing Arguments in Minor Homicide Case 81

The case of Zhou Gu, the adoptive grandmother of Zhou Xinzhen in the Third District, Xiaoyuan Village, poisoning her four-year-old adopted grandson Zhou Tianrong, was publicly tried in the criminal court yesterday. Zhou Gu and Zhou Xingdi, who were in custody, were brought in to await trial. The plaintiff, Zhou Hexi, hired lawyers Lian Oujin and Yu Fan to defend him. Magistrate Liu opened the court. First, Zhou Hexi testified regarding the charge of restricting freedom, stating that Chunxiang was a regular employee and there was no transaction of selling her. The prosecutor's charge of enslaving a person was unacceptable. He further testified that Zhou Gu indeed poisoned Tianrong and requested the court to impose the death penalty according to the law. Next, Zhou Gu and her daughter Zhou Xingdi testified, firmly denying any intention to harm the child. They claimed that Tianrong fell and became ill on July 23rd of last year and died from fright. Subsequently, Zhou Gu's defense lawyers, Sun Xicheng and Tang Ying, stood up and argued that Chunxiang's testimony regarding the poisoning was contradictory and unreliable and should not be adopted. After vigorous debate by the plaintiff's lawyers, Jin and Lian, the court announced the closing of arguments and scheduled the verdict for 2 PM on the 31st of this month. The defendants, Zhou Gu and Zhou Xingdi, were returned to custody.

Changzhou Youth Commits Suicide in Wuxi 82

Qian Weiru, a 24-year-old youth from Changzhou, graduated from middle school and worked for an advertising company, but soon quit. Being unemployed at home, he repeatedly sought work but failed. He became depressed and unhappy. He was further mocked by his two elder brothers, which made him feel he had no reason to live. He came to Wuxi the day before yesterday, checked into Room 17 of the Xin Travel Agency on the road, and left the next morning. He did not return until 10 PM, when he swallowed a bottle of Lysol and committed suicide. The hotel staff noticed and immediately reported it to the front desk. He was sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, he had taken a small amount of poison, and his life was not in danger. Yesterday (the 25th), Weiru's father, Qian Yaoqiu, came to Wuxi from Changzhou to visit him in the hospital and took his son back to recover.

Changshu: Director of Agricultural Cooperative Detained for Embezzlement 83

The Farmers Bank has a farmer's warehouse in Wangshi Town, which is managed by Cheng Xingwu, a local party member. The Farmers Bank recently discovered that he had embezzled 1,200 yuan of cooperative funds that Huang Wei had returned, without paying a single penny, and then disappeared. He secretly returned to Changshu a few days ago and stayed at the Daxin Hotel in front of the temple. The Farmers Bank found out, reported him to the police, and had him arrested. He was handed over to the county court for interrogation yesterday. As a result of the interrogation, he was ordered to repay in installments. Since Cheng was unable to pay the first installment of the embezzled funds, he was taken into custody. It was found that Cheng used to be a member of the county party headquarters' supervisory committee and had been expelled from the party for a previous case.

Nantong: Issue of Detaining Opium Offenders 84

The counties under the jurisdiction of the Nantong District have carried out a general crackdown on opium offenders. A large number of male and female offenders have been apprehended. The detention centers are overcrowded, and the rehabilitation centers are also full. After sentencing, a portion of the offenders will be sent to opium addicts' factories to learn skills, while the rest should be sent to prison. However, the prisons are already crowded with prisoners sent from neighboring counties and cannot accommodate them. After consultation, the county magistrates have telegraphed the province for instructions.

Attempt to Visit Daughter Turns into Knife Attack 85

Hu Shanfu, the owner of Runquan Wine Shop on Xidajie Street in Tongcheng, had many concubines because he had no sons. Zhu Shixia from Shandong, after his daughter became Hu's concubine, was unable to see her. Enraged, he carried a sharp knife to the shop to kill Hu Runshanfu. Hu fled in terror and was stabbed in the arm while tripping at the intersection. Fortunately, the police rescued him, and Zhu Shixia was sent to the court for interrogation and detention.

Hangzhou: Dispatching Personnel to Inspect Dangerous Seawall 86

Due to the lack of major repairs for a long time, the Hangzhou-Pingduan seawall is in a dangerous situation. Sections from the first and second districts, Du to Qi, have become tilted due to the impact of the spring tide, and cracks have been found at the bottom of the seawall. The Water Conservancy Bureau has repeatedly requested the Construction Department to allocate funds for necessary repairs to prevent danger. The Construction Department has specially dispatched Inspector Rao Dongjiu, who is scheduled to depart today (the 26th) with engineer Chen Liyi from the section for inspection, so that the funds can be approved and construction can begin as soon as possible.

Xiaoshan: Large Group of Northern Jiangsu Refugees Seizes Rice 87

On the morning of the 23rd, a large group of Northern Jiangsu refugees suddenly arrived in Kanshan Town, Xiaoshan. More than 100 people were carrying long poles. One group went to Waisha, and another group stopped at the Kanshan dam. The refugees demanded rice from the Zhou Heji rice shop on the dam. When they did not get what they wanted, they looted five shi and five dou of white rice from the shop and left. After receiving the report, the Kanshan Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched a large number of armed police officers to arrest them. Three or four refugees who had fled with the rice were apprehended and taken to the bureau for strict handling.

Education Broadcasting Supplement

Youth and Society (Part 2) - Professor Sun Bentu, College of Liberal Arts, National Central University 88

China is fundamentally a vast nation. Although China is nominally a republic of five ethnicities – Han, Manchu, Mongol, Hui, and Tibetan – in terms of culture, aside from a small minority with some differences in religion and language, the entire country shares the same language, writing system, beliefs, and customs. Therefore, it is a unified, vast nation. In terms of population, it reaches 475 million, accounting for one-fourth of the world's population. Such a large nation governing a country with vast territory and abundant resources is unprecedented in world history. This is the third point we should commend.

In summary, a long history, a vast nation, and a self-contained, distinctive culture are inherent glorious achievements of Chinese society and are worthy of our praise. Our youth, recognizing these inherent glorious achievements, should strive to promote and carry them forward. This is the first responsibility.

Second, they bear the responsibility of building the future of society. Youth not only bear the responsibility of promoting the inherent glorious achievements of society but also the responsibility of correcting the inherent shortcomings of society. To correct inherent shortcomings, it is necessary to adopt the characteristic cultures of Europe and America to adapt to the needs of the times. Therefore, Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, "After restoring all our national essence, we must also learn from the strengths of Europe and America to be able to compete with them."

Since China's communication with Europe and America, European and American culture has been continuously imported. As a result, society has undergone rapid changes. The inherent Chinese culture, which was previously regarded as the sole standard of society, has gradually begun to waver. European and American culture has penetrated all aspects of Chinese life. Not only has the new culture that our country lacked been widely introduced, but our excellent spiritual culture has also been greatly affected. If this trend continues without reversing the tide of Europeanization, China will be completely Europeanized, replacing our inherent special culture. We must know that if a country cannot retain its inherent special culture, then the country's life is very dangerous, because a country's unique special culture is where its national soul resides. Moreover, how can we allow the special culture in which our national soul is rooted to be shaken by foreign cultures when our country has such a long history and such a vast nation? Of course, we should learn from the strengths of Europe and America to compensate for our shortcomings, but at the same time, we should preserve our inherent strengths and allow them to flourish. This is the responsibility of youth. Generally speaking, China's strengths lie in morality, philosophy, art, writing, and so on. And the inherent special culture that I mentioned above is the "national soul" culture formed with inherent morality and philosophy as the backbone. Europe and America's strengths lie in science. Natural science has produced modern machine culture; social science has produced modern political, economic, and educational organizational cultures. The new construction of Chinese society in the future should take China's inherent special culture as the backbone, as the foundation, and the scientific culture, machine culture, and organizational culture of Europe and America as branches and leaves, as nutrients. The New Life Movement and the National Economic Construction Movement advocated by President Chiang are construction movements to promote inherent culture and develop scientific culture. The central responsibility for this new construction movement lies with our youth.

Third, the cultivation that youth should have

From the above, youth are so important in society, and youth have such great responsibilities to society. Then, how should they cultivate themselves so that they can be worthy of their position and bear this great responsibility? In my opinion, first, they should cultivate a sound personality; second, they should strengthen their physical health; and third, they should master specialized knowledge and skills.

First, cultivating a sound personality is the foundation of all endeavors. The achievement of great undertakings must be based on a sound personality. This sound personality has genuine value. It cannot be falsely decorated by oneself, nor can it be destroyed by others. Of course, in a turbulent world, upright people are often slandered by others because right and wrong are unclear. However, if a person truly has a sound personality with genuine value, then even if they are temporarily slandered by others, there will eventually be a day when right and wrong become clear. Therefore, youth should cultivate a sound personality with genuine value. In detail, a sound personality must have at least eight spirits.

The spirit of self-governance. People must have the spirit of self-governance. This spirit is what the ancients called self-restraint. All human virtues are mostly cultivated from the effort of self-restraint.

The spirit of self-improvement. People must have the spirit of continuous self-improvement. This spirit enables people not to be subdued by the reality of the environment but to struggle forward. All progress in life comes from this spirit.

The scientific spirit. People must cultivate the spirit of a scientist. Scientists are most full of the spirits of perseverance, caution, courage, and dedication. This spirit is the element of success in all endeavors.

The spirit of labor. People must have the spirit of hard work and endurance. All success in life comes from labor.

The spirit of justice. People must have the spirit of fighting for justice. Where there is justice, there is no room for complacency. Mencius said, "Wealth and honor cannot corrupt him, poverty and meanness cannot move him, and power and force cannot subdue him." This is the manifestation of the spirit of justice.

The spirit of solidarity. People must have the spirit of unity with society. Because individuals in society share weal and woe with the whole society, they must cooperate and help each other and unite sincerely in order to promote social progress. However, if abnormal solidarity is sufficient to harm social order and social morality, then, for the sake of maintaining justice, one should not associate with it.

The spirit of service. Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, "The purpose of life is service." He also said, "Service is the new morality of the world." Therefore, the general youth should have the spirit of serving society to increase the welfare of the people.

Aspiration—a fundamental spirit. Aspiration is the foundation of success. If a person cannot set aspirations, then even if they have the various spirits mentioned above, they still cannot achieve great undertakings. Therefore, Zeng Guofan said, "The first thing in life is to have aspirations."

Second, one must cultivate a healthy body. People must have a healthy body. With a healthy body, coupled with the cultivation of personality and the mastery of knowledge and skills, one can undertake great things. As the saying goes, "A sound mind resides in a sound body." This sentence is indeed correct.

Third, one must master specialized knowledge and skills. People must have specialized knowledge and skills, so that they can either seek a proper profession on a small scale or do great things for the country and society on a large scale. As for what kind of specialized knowledge and skills should be mastered, it is entirely up to one's own choice.

Only with a healthy body, a sound personality, and specialized knowledge and skills can youth shoulder the responsibility for society. This responsibility is to promote our country's inherent special culture and glorious history on the one hand, and to absorb the characteristic cultures of Europe and America to build a new culture that meets the needs of the times on the other hand. In this way, the revival of the entire Chinese nation can be promoted. Mr. Sun Yat-sen once told his comrades, "The revolution has not yet succeeded, and comrades still need to work hard." I am now imitating this sentence to respectfully tell the youth: "The nation is waiting to be revived, and the youth must work hard." (The End)

Mayor Wu Resigns from Concurrent Post; Yang Hu Succeeds as Songhu Garrison Commander 89

Security Office Reorganized into Security General Corps

Inauguration Ceremony Scheduled for the 28th

Since Mayor Wu Tiecheng resigned from the concurrent post of Songhu Garrison Commander of this city, Chairman Chiang has selected Yang Xiaotian, the Director of the Municipal Security Office, to succeed him. The official order has already arrived in Shanghai. After receiving the order, Yang has scheduled the inauguration ceremony for the 28th of this month. The details are reported as follows:

Yang Hu Succeeds

The post of Songhu Garrison Commander has always been held concurrently by Mayor Wu Tiecheng. Now, Mayor Wu, considering the heavy municipal affairs of Shanghai and his inability to attend to both, specially telegraphed Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission to earnestly resign from the concurrent post, so as to concentrate on the prosperity of Greater Shanghai. His request was approved, and Yang Xiaotian, the Director of the Municipal Security Office, was selected to succeed him. The official order arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning.

Yang's Remarks

After the news of Yang's succession as Songhu Garrison Commander was released, the reporter interviewed Yang at the Security Office headquarters in Fenglinqiao. He was granted an audience and said that he deeply felt the importance of his duties as Songhu Garrison Commander. During Mayor Wu's concurrent term, the order was maintained and the people lived in peace, all thanks to Wu's skillful management. He expressed his deep admiration for Mayor Wu's leadership as the director of the Security Office. Now that he has been ordered to succeed to the important task of Songhu Garrison Commander, he will follow Mayor Wu's intentions and continue his policies, hoping not to fail in his duties, etc.

Yang's Brief Biography

Lieutenant General Yang Hu, also known as Yang Xiaotian, is 49 years old and hails from Ningguo, Anhui. He is a veteran revolutionary general who has served alongside the late Premier, Martyr Chen Yingshi, and Chairman Chiang for many years, participating in numerous military operations. In the 16th year of the Republic, he served as the Director of the Special Affairs Office of the General Headquarters of the National Revolutionary Army, a member of the Anhui Provincial Government, the first Songhu Garrison Commander, a Military Counselor to the National Government, a Central Supervisory Committee Member in the Fourth and Fifth sessions, and the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Security Office for many years. He has excellent relationships with both Chinese and foreigners, and is highly praised by all parties. Now, he has once again been appointed as Garrison Commander, and with his experience, his merits will surely be even more evident.

Hurry to Complete

The original Security Office, it is heard, will be reorganized into a Security General Corps. The candidate for the post of General Corps Commander has been confirmed. According to the reporter's inquiry, it is said to be Ji Zhangjian, who is currently in Beijing and has not yet arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, the departments of the Security Office began to rush to complete the preparations.

The purpose is to balance the price of subsidiary coins
